CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a concise summary of resource changes,\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a formatted string representation of the changes in the plan,\n// grouped by action type with summary counts.\nfunc (c *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed objects and no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tactionGroups[rc.Action] = append(actionGroups[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order in which actions should be displayed\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Open,\n\t\tplans.Renew,\n\t\tplans.Close,\n\t}\n\n\t// Counters for summary\n\tvar totalCount int\n\n\t// Format each action group\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action section\n\t\tactionLabel := c.getActionLabel(action)\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\t// Format: \"  resource_type.name\"\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", c.formatResourceAddress(rc.Addr)))\n\t\t\ttotalCount++\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tif totalCount > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Summary: %d resource(s) will be changed\\n\", totalCount))\n\t} else {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"No changes planned\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// getActionLabel returns a human-readable label for an plans.Renew:\n\t\treturn \"Renew\"\n\tcase plans.Close:\n\t\treturn \"Close\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatResourceAddress returns a formatted resource address string\nfunc (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a concise summary of resource changes,\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a formatted string representation of the changes in the plan,\n// grouped by action type with summary counts.\nfunc (c *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed objects and no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tactionGroups[rc.Action] = append(actionGroups[rc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order in which actions should be displayed\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Open,\n\t\tplans.Renew,\n\t\tplans.Close,\n\t}\n\n\t// Counters for summary\n\tvar totalCount int\n\n\t// Format each action group\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action section\n\t\tactionLabel := c.getActionLabel(action)\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\t// Format: \"  resource_type.name\"\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", c.formatResourceAddress(rc.Addr)))\n\t\t\ttotalCount++\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tif totalCount > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Summary: %d resource(s) will be changed\\n\", totalCount))\n\t} else {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"No changes planned\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\treturn buf.String()\n}\n\n// getActionLabel returns a human-readable label for an action\nfunc (c *CompactDiffFormatter) getActionLabel(action plans.Action) string {\n\tswitch action {\n\tcase plans.Create:\n\t\treturn \"Create\"\n\tcase plans.Update:\n\t\treturn \"Update\"\n\tcase plans.Delete:\n\t\treturn \"Delete\"\n\tcase plans.DeleteThenCreate:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (delete then create)\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenDelete:\n\t\treturn \"Replace (create then delete)\"\n\tcase plans.Read:\n\t\treturn \"Read\"\n\tcase plans.Forget:\n\t\treturn \"Forget\"\n\tcase plans.CreateThenForget:\n\t\treturn \"Create then forget\"\n\tcase plans.Open:\n\t\treturn \"Open\"\n\tcase plans.Renew:\n\t\treturn \"Renew\"\n\tcase plans.Close:\n\t\treturn \"Close\"\n\tdefault:\n\t\treturn \"Unknown\"\n\t}\n}\n\n// formatResourceAddress returns a formatted resource address string\nfunc SPDX-License-Identifier: BUSL-1.1\n\npackage format\n\nimport (\n\t\"bytes\"\n\t\"fmt\"\n\t\"sort\"\n\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/addrs\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/plans\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/schemarepo\"\n\t\"github.com/hashicorp/terraform/internal/states\"\n)\n\n// CompactDiffFormatter formats a plan as a concise summary of resource changes,\n// showing only resource-level changes without attribute-level detail.\ntype CompactDiffFormatter struct{}\n\n// Format returns a formatted string representation of the changes in the plan,\n// grouped by action type with summary counts.\nfunc (c *CompactDiffFormatter) Format(plan *plans.Plan, schemas *schemarepo.Schemas) string {\n\tif plan == nil || plan.Changes == nil {\n\t\treturn \"\"\n\t}\n\n\tvar buf bytes.Buffer\n\n\t// Group resources by action\n\tactionGroups := make(map[plans.Action][]*plans.ResourceInstanceChangeSrc)\n\tfor _, rc := range plan.Changes.Resources {\n\t\t// Skip deposed objects and no-op changes\n\t\tif rc.DeposedKey != states.NotDeposed || rc.ChangeSrc.Action == plans.NoOp {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tactionGroups[rc.ChangeSrc.Action] = append(actionGroups[rc.ChangeSrc.Action], rc)\n\t}\n\n\t// Define the order in which actions should be displayed\n\tactionOrder := []plans.Action{\n\t\tplans.Create,\n\t\tplans.Update,\n\t\tplans.DeleteThenCreate,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenDelete,\n\t\tplans.Delete,\n\t\tplans.Read,\n\t\tplans.Forget,\n\t\tplans.CreateThenForget,\n\t\tplans.Open,\n\t\tplans.Renew,\n\t\tplans.Close,\n\t}\n\n\t// Counters for summary\n\tvar totalCount int\n\n\t// Format each action group\n\tfor _, action := range actionOrder {\n\t\tresources, ok := actionGroups[action]\n\t\tif !ok || len(resources) == 0 {\n\t\t\tcontinue\n\t\t}\n\n\t\t// Sort resources by address for consistent output\n\t\tsort.Slice(resources, func(i, j int) bool {\n\t\t\treturn resources[i].Addr.String() < resources[j].Addr.String()\n\t\t})\n\n\t\t// Write action section\n\t\tactionLabel := c.getActionLabel(action)\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"%s:\\n\", actionLabel))\n\n\t\tfor _, rc := range resources {\n\t\t\t// Format: \"  resource_type.name\"\n\t\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"  %s\\n\", c.formatResourceAddress(rc.Addr)))\n\t\t\ttotalCount++\n\t\t}\n\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(\"\\n\")\n\t}\n\n\t// Write summary\n\tif totalCount > 0 {\n\t\tbuf.WriteString(fmt.Sprintf(\"Summary: %d
